\#0 load functions and packages

\#1 Introduction To estimate mean priors from the separate interval
groups (the short and long ranges, and mixed ranges. we adopted the left
and right spatial separation for the short and long ranges, as used in
Roach et al.~(2017).

\begin{figure}
\centering
\includegraphics[width=0.6\textwidth,height=\textheight]{images/timeline.png}
\caption{Procedure}
\end{figure}

\#\#3.1 Experiment 1

In exp1, the target intervals are the ramdomly selected elements from
three groups of time intervals: group short (400-800ms), group long
(1200-1600ms), and a mixed group(400-800ms, 1200-1600ms).

The experiment consisted of three sessions with each had 160 trials. The
time intervals in short group are 400, 475.7, 565.7, 672.7, 800ms. The
time intervals in long group are 1.2, 1.4, 1.9, 2.02, and 2.4s. The
short and long ranges were separated by 400 ms. The order between short
group and long group was counterbalanced across participants. The mixed
group is always the last session.

In exp1, there are one practice block and 24 formal blocks. Each block
has 20 trials. The duration of the circle displayed on the screen is the
interval that participants need to replicate. By pressing left button
(Mouse) to reproduce the time duration as long as stimulus was
presented. Participants received feedback after their response.

In Exp1, the intervals from short-range were spaced logarithmically
between 400 and 800 ms, with a mean of 583 ms, a standard deviation (SD)
of 142.2 ms; the intervals from long-range were spaced logarithmically
between 1200 and 2400 ms, with a mean of 1752ms and a standard deviation
(SD) of 427.0 ms; distribution of intervals for the mix session had a
mean of 1166ms and a standard deviation (SD) of 665.5ms.

\hypertarget{central-tendency-analysis}{%
\subsubsection{Central tendency
analysis}\label{central-tendency-analysis}}

It is a reproduction task, so first we examine the reproduction error
and the central tendency effect. We plot two types of colors separately,
and separate for individual subjects.

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]

\includegraphics{1Report_files/figure-latex/unnamed-chunk-17-1.pdf}

\#\#3.2 Experiment 2

In this experiment, the short and long ranges were clearly separate. The
experiment consisted of three sessions with each had 160 trials. The
time intervals used in Exp.2 in short group were chosen from 491.2,
542.9, 600, 663, 732.8 ms, and target intervals in long group were
chosen from 1.31, 1.45, 1.60, 1.77 and 1.954s. The short (491.2-732.8ms)
and long (1310-1954ms) ranges were separated by 577 ms. The order
between short group and long group was counterbalanced across
participants. The mixed group is always the last session.

In exp2, there are one practice block and 16 formal blocks. Each block
has 30 trials. The duration of the circle displayed on the screen is the
interval that participants need to replicate. By pressing left button
(Mouse) to reproduce the time duration as long as stimulus was
presented. Participants received feedback after their response.

\hypertarget{rp-difference-between-ir-and-br}{%
\subsection{RP difference between IR and
BR}\label{rp-difference-between-ir-and-br}}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\#calculate the difference between IR and BR }
\NormalTok{sumexpSub\_diff }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ dplyr}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{select}\NormalTok{(sumexpSub, NSub, targetDur, Exp, priortype, range, m\_err, m\_RP, sd\_err, sd\_RP)}\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
    \FunctionTok{unite}\NormalTok{(values, m\_err, m\_RP, sd\_err, sd\_RP)}\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
    \FunctionTok{spread}\NormalTok{(priortype, values)}\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
    \FunctionTok{separate}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{\textasciigrave{}}\AttributeTok{IR}\StringTok{\textasciigrave{}}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"IR\_err"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"IR\_RP"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"IR\_sd\_err"}\NormalTok{,}\StringTok{"IR\_sd\_RP"}\NormalTok{), }\AttributeTok{sep =} \StringTok{"\_"}\NormalTok{)}\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
    \FunctionTok{separate}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{\textasciigrave{}}\AttributeTok{BR}\StringTok{\textasciigrave{}}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"BR\_err"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"BR\_RP"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"BR\_sd\_err"}\NormalTok{,}\StringTok{"BR\_sd\_RP"}\NormalTok{), }\AttributeTok{sep =} \StringTok{"\_"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{sumexpSub\_diff}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{IR\_err }\OtherTok{=} \FunctionTok{as.numeric}\NormalTok{(sumexpSub\_diff}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{IR\_err)}
\NormalTok{sumexpSub\_diff}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{BR\_err }\OtherTok{=} \FunctionTok{as.numeric}\NormalTok{(sumexpSub\_diff}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{BR\_err)}
\NormalTok{sumexpSub\_diff}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{IR\_RP }\OtherTok{=} \FunctionTok{as.numeric}\NormalTok{(sumexpSub\_diff}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{IR\_RP)}
\NormalTok{sumexpSub\_diff}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{BR\_RP }\OtherTok{=} \FunctionTok{as.numeric}\NormalTok{(sumexpSub\_diff}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{BR\_RP)}
\NormalTok{sumexpSub\_diff}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{IR\_sd\_err }\OtherTok{=} \FunctionTok{as.numeric}\NormalTok{(sumexpSub\_diff}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{IR\_sd\_err)}
\NormalTok{sumexpSub\_diff}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{BR\_sd\_err }\OtherTok{=} \FunctionTok{as.numeric}\NormalTok{(sumexpSub\_diff}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{BR\_sd\_err)}
\NormalTok{sumexpSub\_diff}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{IR\_sd\_RP }\OtherTok{=} \FunctionTok{as.numeric}\NormalTok{(sumexpSub\_diff}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{IR\_sd\_RP)}
\NormalTok{sumexpSub\_diff}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{BR\_sd\_RP }\OtherTok{=} \FunctionTok{as.numeric}\NormalTok{(sumexpSub\_diff}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{BR\_sd\_RP)}

\#\#3.3 Experiment 3

In this experiment, the short and long ranges were clearly separate. The
experiment consisted of three sessions with each had 160 trials. The
time intervals used in Exp.2 in short group were chosen from 491.2,
542.9, 600, 663, 732.8 ms, and target intervals in long group were
chosen from 1.31, 1.45, 1.60, 1.77 and 1.954s. The short (491.2-732.8ms)
and long (1310-1954ms) ranges were separated by 577 ms. The order
between short group and long group was counterbalanced across
participants. The mixed group is always the last session.

In exp2, there are one practice block and 16 formal blocks. Each block
has 30 trials. The duration of the circle displayed on the screen is the
interval that participants need to replicate. By pressing left button
(Mouse) to reproduce the time duration as long as stimulus was
presented. Participants received feedback after their response.

\#\#4.2 observed CV for each subject

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]

\#\#4.6 slopes and indifference points

\hypertarget{slopes-and-ci-categoried-by-3-sessionsshort-long-mix}{%
\subsubsection{slopes and CI categoried by 3 sessions(short, long,
mix)}\label{slopes-and-ci-categoried-by-3-sessionsshort-long-mix}}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{slope\_group }\OtherTok{=}\NormalTok{ exps}\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}\NormalTok{ dplyr}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{group\_by}\NormalTok{(NSub, Exp, group) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} \FunctionTok{nest}\NormalTok{()  }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} 
    \FunctionTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{model =} \FunctionTok{map}\NormalTok{(data, mRep\_model)) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}  \CommentTok{\# linear regression}
    \FunctionTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{slope =} \FunctionTok{map}\NormalTok{(model, broom}\SpecialCharTok{::}\NormalTok{tidy)) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}  \CommentTok{\# get estimates}
    \FunctionTok{unnest}\NormalTok{(slope, }\AttributeTok{.drop =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} \CommentTok{\# remove raw data}
    \FunctionTok{select}\NormalTok{(}\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\NormalTok{std.error,}\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\NormalTok{statistic, }\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\NormalTok{p.value) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}  \CommentTok{\# remove unnessary columns}
    \FunctionTok{spread}\NormalTok{(term, estimate) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}   \CommentTok{\# spread stimates}
\NormalTok{    dplyr}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{rename}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{minRP =} \StringTok{\textasciigrave{}}\AttributeTok{(Intercept)}\StringTok{\textasciigrave{}}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{slope =}\NormalTok{ targetDur)  }\CommentTok{\# rename columns}
\NormalTok{slope\_group}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{data }\OtherTok{=} \ConstantTok{NULL}
\NormalTok{slope\_group}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{model }\OtherTok{=} \ConstantTok{NULL}
\NormalTok{slope\_group}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{inP }\OtherTok{=}\NormalTok{ slope\_group}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{minRP}\SpecialCharTok{/}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{1}\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\NormalTok{slope\_group}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{slope)}
\NormalTok{slope\_group}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{CI}\OtherTok{=} \DecValTok{1}\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\NormalTok{slope\_group}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{slope}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\#\#4.10 Estimated InP with bootstrapped 95\% confidence intervals

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\#calculate the bootstrapped 95\% confidence intervals }
\NormalTok{generateCI }\OtherTok{=} \ConstantTok{FALSE} \CommentTok{\# tag for generation CI}
\ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{(generateCI)\{}
\NormalTok{  cilist }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \ConstantTok{NULL}
\NormalTok{  my\_data }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ exps}\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} \FunctionTok{select}\NormalTok{(NSub, Exp, priortype, range, RP, targetDur)}
  \ControlFlowTok{for}\NormalTok{(expname }\ControlFlowTok{in} \FunctionTok{unique}\NormalTok{(exps}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{Exp))\{}
    \ControlFlowTok{for}\NormalTok{(prior }\ControlFlowTok{in} \FunctionTok{unique}\NormalTok{(exps}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{priortype))\{}
      \ControlFlowTok{for}\NormalTok{(group }\ControlFlowTok{in} \FunctionTok{unique}\NormalTok{(exps}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{range))\{}
        \ControlFlowTok{for}\NormalTok{(nsub }\ControlFlowTok{in} \FunctionTok{unique}\NormalTok{(exps}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{NSub))\{}
\NormalTok{          dat }\OtherTok{=}\NormalTok{ my\_data }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} \FunctionTok{filter}\NormalTok{(Exp }\SpecialCharTok{==}\NormalTok{ expname, priortype }\SpecialCharTok{==}\NormalTok{ prior, range }\SpecialCharTok{==}\NormalTok{ group, NSub }\SpecialCharTok{==}\NormalTok{ nsub)}
          \FunctionTok{set.seed}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{100}\NormalTok{) }
          \CommentTok{\# Calling the boot function with the dataset }
          \CommentTok{\# our function and no. of rounds }
\NormalTok{          num }\OtherTok{=} \DecValTok{1000}\NormalTok{;}
\NormalTok{          bs\_InP }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{boot}\NormalTok{(dat, getInP, }\AttributeTok{R =}\NormalTok{ num) }
\NormalTok{          bs\_Slope }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{boot}\NormalTok{(dat, getBootSlope,  }\AttributeTok{R =}\NormalTok{ num )}
\NormalTok{          bs\_Intercept }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{boot}\NormalTok{(dat, getIntercept, }\AttributeTok{R =}\NormalTok{ num)}
\NormalTok{          ci }\OtherTok{=} \FunctionTok{data.frame}\NormalTok{(}
            \AttributeTok{Exp =}\NormalTok{ expname,}
            \AttributeTok{priortype =}\NormalTok{ prior,}
            \AttributeTok{range =}\NormalTok{ group,}
            \AttributeTok{NSub =}\NormalTok{ nsub,}
            \AttributeTok{sdInP =} \FunctionTok{sd}\NormalTok{(bs\_InP}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{t),}
            \AttributeTok{mInP =} \FunctionTok{median}\NormalTok{(bs\_InP}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{t),}
            \AttributeTok{mSlope =} \FunctionTok{median}\NormalTok{(bs\_Slope}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{t),}
            \AttributeTok{sdSlope =} \FunctionTok{sd}\NormalTok{(bs\_Slope}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{t),}
            \AttributeTok{mIntercept =} \FunctionTok{median}\NormalTok{(bs\_Intercept}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{t),}
            \AttributeTok{sdIntercept =} \FunctionTok{sd}\NormalTok{(bs\_Intercept}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{t)}
\NormalTok{          )}
\NormalTok{          cilist }\OtherTok{=} \FunctionTok{data.frame}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{rbind}\NormalTok{(cilist, ci))}
\NormalTok{        \}}
\NormalTok{      \}}
\NormalTok{    \}}
\NormalTok{  \}}
  \FunctionTok{write.csv}\NormalTok{(cilist, }\AttributeTok{file =} \FunctionTok{paste0}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"generated/ci\_list\_median\_1000.csv"}\NormalTok{))}
\NormalTok{\}}
\end{Highlighting}

\hypertarget{mean-indifference-poinst-based-on-group}{%
\paragraph{mean indifference poinst based on
group}\label{mean-indifference-poinst-based-on-group}}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\#based on group}
\NormalTok{cilist }\OtherTok{=} \FunctionTok{data.frame}\NormalTok{(cilist, }\AttributeTok{stringsAsFactors=}\ConstantTok{FALSE}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{cilist}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{group }\OtherTok{=}\NormalTok{ cilist}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{range}
\FunctionTok{levels}\NormalTok{(cilist}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{group) }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{\textquotesingle{}long\textquotesingle{}}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{\textquotesingle{}short\textquotesingle{}}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{\textquotesingle{}mixed\textquotesingle{}}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{cilist[}\FunctionTok{which}\NormalTok{(cilist}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{priortype }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"IR"}\NormalTok{), }\StringTok{"group"}\NormalTok{] }\OtherTok{=} \StringTok{\textquotesingle{}mixed\textquotesingle{}}
 
\NormalTok{mCI\_gr }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ cilist}\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} \FunctionTok{group\_by}\NormalTok{(Exp, group) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
\NormalTok{  dplyr}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{summarise}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{n =} \FunctionTok{n}\NormalTok{(),}
                   \AttributeTok{ci\_InP\_upper =}\FunctionTok{CI}\NormalTok{(mInP,}\AttributeTok{ci=}\FloatTok{0.95}\NormalTok{)[}\StringTok{"upper"}\NormalTok{],}
                   \AttributeTok{ci\_InP\_mean =} \FunctionTok{CI}\NormalTok{(mInP,}\AttributeTok{ci=}\FloatTok{0.95}\NormalTok{)[}\StringTok{"mean"}\NormalTok{],}
                   \AttributeTok{ci\_InP\_lower =} \FunctionTok{CI}\NormalTok{(mInP,}\AttributeTok{ci=}\FloatTok{0.95}\NormalTok{)[}\StringTok{"lower"}\NormalTok{],}
